2889 /* Delay after an RCC peripheral clock enabling */ \
2890 tmpreg = READ_BIT(RCC->AHB1ENR, RCC_AHB1ENR_GPIODEN);\
2891 UNUSED(tmpreg); \

5737/*------------------------------- PLL Configuration --------------------------*/
5738#if defined(STM32F410Tx) || defined(STM32F410Cx) || defined(STM32F410Rx) || defined(STM32F446xx) ||\
5739 defined(STM32F469xx) || defined(STM32F479xx) || defined(STM32F412Zx) || defined(STM32F412Vx) || \
5740 defined(STM32F412Rx) || defined(STM32F412Cx) || defined(STM32F413xx) || defined(STM32F423xx)
5774#define __HAL_RCC_PLL_CONFIG(__RCC_PLLSource__, __PLLM__, __PLLN__, __PLLP__, __PLLQ__,__PLLR__) \
5775 (RCC->PLLCFGR = ((__RCC_PLLSource__) | (__PLLM__) | \
5776 ((__PLLN__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLN_Pos) | \
5777 ((((__PLLP__) >> 1U) -1U) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLP_Pos) | \
5778 ((__PLLQ__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLQ_Pos) | \
5779 ((__PLLR__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLR_Pos)))
5780#else
5810#define __HAL_RCC_PLL_CONFIG(__RCC_PLLSource__, __PLLM__, __PLLN__, __PLLP__, __PLLQ__) \
5811 (RCC->PLLCFGR = (0x20000000U | (__RCC_PLLSource__) | (__PLLM__)| \
5812 ((__PLLN__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLN_Pos) | \
5813 ((((__PLLP__) >> 1U) -1U) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLP_Pos) | \
5814 ((__PLLQ__) << RCC_PLLCFGR_PLLQ_Pos)))
5815 #endif /* STM32F410xx || STM32F446xx || STM32F469xx || STM32F479xx || STM32F412Zx || STM32F412Vx || STM32F412Rx || STM32F412Cx */
